function GetDate(id) {\n        var joindate = $(id).datepicker('getDate');\n\n        return joindate;\n    }\n\n    function MinimumCheckInDate() {\n        return GetDate('#DefaultCheckinDate');\n    }\n\n    function MaximumCheckInDate() {\n        var currDate = new Date(Date.now());\n        var maxCheckInDate = GetDate('#MaxCheckinDate');\n        if (maxCheckInDate > currDate) {\n            return GetDate('#MaxCheckinDate');\n        } else {\n            return new Date($('#MaxCheckinDate').datepicker('getDate'));\n        }\n    }\n\n    function MinimumCheckOutDate() {\n        var joindate = GetDate('#CheckinDate');\n\n        if (joindate == null) {\n            joindate = MinimumCheckInDate();\n        }\n\n        var minDaysForCheckIn = parseInt($('#MinimumNumberOfNights').val());\n\n        var stayDuration = parseInt($('#MinStayDuration').val());\n\n        if (joindate != null) {\n            if (!isNaN(stayDuration)) {\n                joindate.setDate(joindate.getDate() + stayDuration);\n            }\n            else if (!isNaN(minDaysForCheckIn)) {\n                joindate.setDate(joindate.getDate() + minDaysForCheckIn);\n            }\n        }\n        return joindate;\n    };\n\n    function MaximumCheckOutDate() {\n        var joindate = null;\n        var stayDuration = parseInt($('#MaxStayDuration').val());\n\n        if (!isNaN(stayDuration)) {\n            joindate = GetDate('#CheckinDate');\n            joindate = joindate == null ? MinimumCheckInDate() : joindate;\n            joindate.setDate(joindate.getDate() + stayDuration);\n        }\n\n        return joindate;\n    }\n\n    function SetMinimumMaximumCheckOutDate() {\n        $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker('option', 'minDate', MinimumCheckOutDate());\n        $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker('option', 'maxDate', MaximumCheckOutDate());\n\n        $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker('setDate', MinimumCheckOutDate());\n    }\n\n    function CheckStayDuration() {\n        var minStayDuration = parseInt($('#MinStayDuration').val());\n        var maxStayDuration = parseInt($('#MaxStayDuration').val());\n\n        if (!isNaN(minStayDuration) && !isNaN(maxStayDuration)) {\n            if (minStayDuration == maxStayDuration) {\n                $('#CheckoutDate').attr('readonly', 'readonly');\n                $('#CheckoutDate').css('background-color', 'rgb(204, 204, 204)');\n                $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker('option', 'showOn', 'off');\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    function CheckCheckInDate(event) {\n        if (event.which === $.ui.keyCode.ENTER || event.which === $.ui.keyCode.TAB) {\n            var checkinDate = GetDate('#CheckinDate');\n\n            if (checkinDate == null) {\n                checkinDate = MinimumCheckInDate();\n            }\n\n            $('#CheckinDate').datepicker('setDate', checkinDate);\n            $(this).datepicker('hide');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function CheckCheckOutDate(event) {\n        if (event.which === $.ui.keyCode.ENTER || event.which === $.ui.keyCode.TAB) {\n            var checkoutDate = GetDate('#CheckoutDate');\n\n            if (checkoutDate == null) {\n                checkoutDate = MinimumCheckOutDate();\n            }\n\n            $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker('setDate', checkoutDate);\n            $(this).datepicker('hide');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function CheckDestinationDropDown() {\n        var destinationOptions = $('#Destination option')\n                                    .not('[value=\"\"]')\n                                    .not('[value|=\"CONTINENT\"]')\n                                    .not('[value|=\"COUNTRY\"]')\n                                    .not('[value|=\"STATE\"]')\n                                    .not('[value|=\"REGION\"]')\n                                    .not('[value|=\"COUNTRYREGION\"]');\n        if (destinationOptions.length == 1) {\n            $('#Destination').empty();\n            $('#Destination').append(destinationOptions[0]);\n            $('#Destination').css('background-color', 'rgb(204, 204, 204)');\n        }\n    }\n\n    $(document).ready(function () {\n\n        $('#CheckinDate').datepicker('option', {\n            minDate: MinimumCheckInDate(),\n            maxDate: MaximumCheckInDate(),\n            onSelect: function () {\n                SetMinimumMaximumCheckOutDate();\n                $('#CheckinDate').blur();\n                $('#CheckoutDate').blur();\n            }\n        });\n\n        $('#CheckinDate').focus(function () { $('#CheckinDate').blur(); });\n\n        $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker('option', {\n            minDate: MinimumCheckOutDate(),\n            maxDate: MaximumCheckOutDate(),\n            onSelect: function () {\n                $('#CheckoutDate').blur();\n            }\n        });\n\n        $('#CheckoutDate').focus(function () { $('#CheckoutDate').blur(); });\n\n        $('#CheckinDate').datepicker().keydown(CheckCheckInDate);\n        $('#CheckoutDate').datepicker().keydown(CheckCheckOutDate);\n\n        $.fn.modal.Constructor.prototype.enforceFocus = function () { };\n       \n        $('#cmdSearchResortsFeatureTabSubmit').click(function (e) {\n            if ($('#searchFeatureForm').valid()) {\n                if ($('#searchFeature').hasClass('modal')) {\n                    if ($('#searchFeature').data('bs.modal') && $('#searchFeature').data('bs.modal').isShown)\n                        $('#searchFeature').modal(\"hide\");\n                }\n                if ($('#searchFeatureBox').hasClass('modal')) {\n                    if ($('#searchFeatureBox').data('bs.modal') && $('#searchFeatureBox').data('bs.modal').isShown)\n                        $('#searchFeatureBox').modal(\"hide\");\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        CheckStayDuration();\n        CheckDestinationDropDown();\n    });\n</script>\n\n
